class="sc-kfWwvt gdRcDB"><div style="min-height: 80px;"><div class="markdown-converter__text--rendered"><p>This dataset contains 35 classes of wild edible plants with a total of 16,535 images. Each class varies in the number of images between 400 to 500. It has been tested with three state-of-the-art CNN architectures: MobileNet v2, GoogLeNet, and ResNet-34 using Transfer Learning.</p>
